Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 9, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/wizardslogo_thumb.jpg)
By Adam Styborski and Marc Calderaro










We know how you kids like the decklists. And Top 8 decklists just aren't enough. There are tons of fantastic decks that could have been in those final few if things broke differently. Below are the decklists from places 9th through 32nd.
